Zhuang Henian, the director of the business department, reported on the operating account of the 20th year. Xu Xiuzhi, the resident inspector, reported that the audit account was consistent. Then, the proposed matters were proposed separately: (1) The profit distribution plan for the 20th year, (2) The payment of dividends, (3) The appropriation of savings reserve fund, (4) The term of office of the directors of the bank has expired, and it is proposed to extend the term and re-elect and reappoint them, (5) The re-election of business shareholders' supervisors were all passed. After that, the supervisors were elected by voting, and the shareholders determined Xu Jiqing and Wang Zihong. The two gentlemen monitored the voting results. Yu Baoxuan, Jia Shiyi, Liang Dingji, and Ye Chongyou received the most votes and were elected as business shareholders' supervisors. Notice Regarding the Anti-Opium Society's Concern Over the Revival of Opium Public Sales

The Chinese National Anti-Opium Society, noting the increasing atmosphere of opium public sales in Fujian and Anhui provinces, and hearing rumors that the central government is also brewing a revival of the public sales system, has issued a declaration urging the nation to pay attention. The original text is recorded below:

[To all compatriots of the nation: Last spring, the internationally shocking opium public sales system, which caused a nationwide sensation, was once implemented. Wu Yulin initiated it, and Li Jihong supported its success. The central financial authorities, misled by its profits, disregarded public opinion and announced its implementation, suppressing the people's spirit. Fortunately, the people's hearts were not dead, and they unanimously rose up in opposition, with overwhelming momentum. The authorities were also intimidated and temporarily retreated, ordering its cancellation. However, everyone knew that this was only a temporary appeasement and not a complete withdrawal. Indeed, before long, the news of Anhui Province establishing a "Prohibition and Investigation Bureau" shocked the country and was widely reported in various newspapers. The central authorities remained silent. Subsequently, the troops stationed in southern Fujian pressured farmers to plant opium and collect taxes, but did the central government not know about this, or did it not care? Recently, Fang Shengtao, the acting chairman of Fujian Province, colluded with the stationed troops to implement opium public sales. The central government remains silent, and although various foreign embassies and consulates have sent urgent telegrams, they have received no response. Chen Diaoyuan and Fang Shengtao, the masterminds behind the public sales in Anhui and Fujian, have not been punished according to the law. Such measures suggest that the central government is intentionally condoning and tacitly approving it. Recently, the atmosphere of public sales has become more prevalent. Reports indicate that the military authorities in North China, due to a lack of military funds, have decided to implement opium public sales. The plan involves establishing a public sales office in each of the provinces of Rehe, Chahar, and Hebei, with Gao Jiyi in charge, expecting a monthly income of two million yuan. Furthermore, anti-opium comrades across the country have sent telegrams reporting that the central government is financially exhausted and misled by proponents of public sales, seeking to exploit the national crisis by cleverly establishing a name to revive the public sales system. Comrades abroad have also reported that the central financial authorities are borrowing a large national debt from a certain country, using the revenue from opium public sales as collateral. Alas, what time is this? What kind of talk is this? What are you gentlemen thinking? At a time when the country is fragmented, foreign troops are rampant, and the survival of the nation is in jeopardy, with the threat of joint administration looming, the authorities should be too busy saving the nation to even consider it. What are they thinking, reviving the old dream of public sales? It seems that the central government has never forgotten this matter since abandoning public sales last year. The reason it has not been immediately revived is only waiting for the right opportunity. If the opium public sales system is truly a good system, why have European and American countries not followed suit during their economic downturns? Why do they not see this as a source of profit, while China is treated like a favored child, enjoying its benefits alone? Why do the colonial policies of major powers use the opium public sales system as a tool to weaken the people's spirit and extract profits? Japan immediately implemented opium public sales in Taiwan, and it is also actively implementing this system in Dalian. Now, after occupying the four northeastern provinces, its first priority is to implement opium public sales, as repeatedly reported in various newspapers. The facts are clear. What do the gentlemen in authority see that they insist on applying the colonial policies used on others to their own people? Is this not digging their own graves? How can people be so unconscionable? This society, entrusted by the will of the whole people, takes pure anti-opium as its stance, regardless of politics or party strife. It only asks that the government does not violate the Premier's policy of complete prohibition and permanently abolish any opium prohibition measures with the nature of public sales. Other political issues are not of concern. If opium must be used as a source of profit, this society will resolutely oppose it, even if it means certain destruction. Now that the talk of reviving public sales has resurfaced, this society cannot shirk its responsibility to fight to the death. We hope that all sectors of the country will pay attention. At a time when the national crisis is urgent and the nation's attention is focused on foreign affairs, it is precisely when villains are advancing their treacherous schemes and using public office for private gain. Either they cleverly establish names to revive public sales, or they blatantly disregard the consequences and implement them. The authorities may not dare to do this, and villains may not dare to come up with this, but the people should be prepared to prevent being deceived and rise up to monitor the authorities and support the prohibition of opium. Do not neglect this harm because the war is not yet over, and do not give those who advocate public sales and unscrupulous officials the opportunity to carry out their evil schemes. The survival of opium prohibition depends on this action. We hope all sectors of society will pay attention to it.

Murder Case Due to Enmity Between Red Cross Members

Xue Zhenyi Hates Hai Zongqi

Three Shots Fired, None Hit Hai

Three Passersby Hit by Stray Bullets

Xue Was Finally Arrested

Hai Zongqi, a Henan native, 32 years old, lives in the lower厢房 of No. 112 Bubenshi Road, French Concession. He is currently the captain of the First Brigade of the Red Cross. Xue Zhenyi (28 years old), from Xuzhou, is also a member of the Red Cross and also holds the position of deputy captain. Recently, Xue was reported by Hai for violating the regulations of the association and was dismissed. Xue hated Hai to the bone and repeatedly thought of revenge, but had no way to do it. Yesterday morning at around 10:00 AM, Xue secretly took a pistol and broke into Hai's bedroom. At that time, Hai had just put on his clothes and was leaving his bed. He caught sight of Xue coming and knew that something was wrong. He asked Xue what he wanted to do. Xue looked fierce and claimed that he needed to borrow 500 yuan for emergency needs. Hai was surprised to hear this and was about to answer when Xue suddenly fired his pistol and shot at Hai three times. Hai dodged in every possible way, and all three bullets hit the glass, sending shards flying. At that time, a tenant upstairs named Wan Yusi heard the sound and suspected it was a robbery, so he shouted for help. Xue saw that the situation was not good and quickly rushed out the door. Hai followed closely. At that time, the French Concession police inspectors Jin Jiulin, 目 Li 龍 Mao Jingen, and Zhang Ziying were passing by on patrol and helped chase after him. When they chased Xue to Beidi Alo Road, Xue turned around and fired several shots to resist arrest. Passersby Gu Fulin, Shen Ruijin, and a seven-year-old girl, Zhu Fuliang, were all injured by stray bullets. Xue fled across Fuxu Road to the intersection of Dagu Road and Chengdu Road. A Chinese police officer, No. 3126, from the Public Concession also joined the chase. As a result, Xue was finally intercepted and taken to the police station. After a detailed interrogation by the police chief, Xue confessed that he currently lived at No. 232 and a half, Rui'an Lane, Shanhai Road. On January 11th, 1928, he was sentenced to two years in prison by the French Court for theft. After being released from prison on January 11th, 1930, he served as a soldier in the 10th Division. In August of last year, he joined the Red Cross as a member. When the January 28th Incident occurred, he changed his position to the rescue team. He admitted to plotting to kill Hai without hesitation. The police chief ordered him to be detained and handed over to the court for strict punishment. The three people injured by stray bullets were temporarily sent to the hospital for treatment and will be investigated after they recover.

The Trial of the Depositor's Appeal in the Ye Shantao Case of the Day and Night Bank Opens

Ye Cannot Evade the Responsibility of a Director

After Huang Chuqiu, the founder of the Day and Night Bank, passed away in the winter of the year before last, the bank announced its liquidation. Subsequently, depositors such as Dong Longxing learned that Ye Shantao, who owned a wealth of real estate and was quite wealthy, was also one of the directors of the bank and should bear corresponding responsibility. Therefore, in the lawsuit, Ye was listed as a defendant. Ye, however, presented a letter signed by Huang Chuqiu allowing him to resign as a director, denying that he was still a director. However, Dong Longxing and others claimed that the letter was forged by Ye and filed a criminal self-accusation against Ye in the First Special District Local Court, demanding that he be punished for the crime of forging documents. After the trial, Ye Shantao was found not guilty. The plaintiffs were unwilling to accept this and hired lawyer Lu Qing to appeal to the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, stating that the defendant presented a letter from Huang Chuqiu to Gan Yuesong as a rebuttal during the initial trial. However, the letter from Huang to Gan was an ordinary letter, which was far from the letter regarding the defendant's resignation as a director, and should not be treated the same. Moreover, after Huang Chuqiu's death, the defendant still served as a member of Huang's aftermath committee. The intention to cover up is quite obvious. During the initial trial, the appellant requested to verify the list of directors and the directors' transportation expenses of the Gongfa Company, which had been submitted to the Third Branch of the Jiangsu High Court, in order to clarify the facts, but it was not adopted. The initial trial summarily judged that Ye Shantao was not guilty, based on the statement that "the defendant presented a letter from Huang Chuqiu to Gan Yuesong and a letter to the defendant, and the跡象 were completely identical," regardless of the nature of the letter. The appellants were unable to accept this and specially filed an appeal, requesting the court to investigate and summon the defendant to court for interrogation, and to revoke the original judgment and punish the defendant for the crime he deserved. Yesterday, the Second Branch of the High Court, with Judge Yu presiding over the trial along with prosecutors Zhao and Guo, heard the case. The lawyer stated the appellant's intention and that the Day and Night Bank belonged to the Gongfa Company, and that the former French Concession Court had determined that the company was indeed a partnership and not a limited company, so shareholders and directors should bear unlimited liability. The defendant's lawyer, Lu Shaozong, claimed that Ye Shantao had also been implicated in the Gongfa lawsuit, but the French court had ruled that Ye was not related. Lawyer Yan continued that the letter was indeed forged by Ye and had no validity, and that Ye's submission of Huang's letter to Gan Yuesong did not conclusively prove anything, and requested that the Second Branch of the High Court obtain the Gongfa accounting books to prove that Ye had received transportation expenses as a director. The presiding judge then announced that the case would be adjourned for further hearing.

Alas, the methods of the Shishi Xinbao can be described as extremely despicable. Recently, we received the good intentions of a gentleman who came forward to mediate. Only yesterday were we able to hold a negotiation with Mr. Ren Jinping, the representative of the newspaper. Our association's attitude has always been calm and restrained. No matter what, we must restore the jobs of the hardworking workers who have served in the newspaper for many years, otherwise we would not care and would leave dozens of families to starve to death. How could we bear it? But Mr. Ren said that the newspaper's will was firm and that restoring the original state was impossible. After repeated consultations, no result could be achieved. Our association, on the one hand, was concerned about the suffering of the forced workers, and on the other hand, needed to explain the unreasonable situation to the newspaper, and even tried our best to tolerate and compromise, but failed to obtain the newspaper's understanding. Now, the forced workers are about to become paupers. Alas, can there be more cruel methods in the world than those of the Shishi Xinbao authorities? Since the establishment of our association to date, we have had five years of struggle history. In these five years, we have always taken labor-capital harmony as our association's motto, and there has never been such a socially alarming labor dispute. Unexpectedly, this time, the Shishi Xinbao thought that our忍 and 求全 could be deceived, and dared to肆意 destroy us regardless of everything. Our association tried our best to avoid conflict, but it was ineffective. However, the right and wrong of things will naturally be corrected by justice. We still hope that all fellow compatriots and workers across the country will give us impartial justice. Even if our association perishes because of the Shishi Xinbao, we can also complain. We declare again,

Free Talk

Anecdotes of Martyr Xiao De

— By Ms. Ye Hua

The people of the nation consider Xiao De to be a martyr. However, few know the anecdotes of the martyr's life. I will record one or two below. The martyr's name was Robert, and he was 26 years old. The outside world says 27, which is wrong. He was from Tacoma, Washington, USA. He loved flying since he was a child and often expressed his thoughts in toys. In his spare time, he would dismantle vacuum cleaners tirelessly, studying their assembly. He dismantled and reassembled them, like a little mechanic. The martyr saw aviation as the first joy in the world and loved airplanes very much. His mother sent him to the Keck Civil Aviation School to suit his personality. After graduation, he also studied military aviation. In the middle of the European War, he joined the Allied forces and made several contributions. In the spring of 1930, he left his mother and home and came to China from the United States. He stayed at No. 150 Jing'an Temple Road in Shanghai. He served as a pilot in the Aviation Department and a flying instructor at the Aviation School of the Ministry of Military Affairs. After coming to China, he had a full of enthusiasm and great hope. He wrote to his home country, often saying that the Chinese nation loves peace, is humble and polite, and he is happy in this land. Therefore, his mother repeatedly called him back, but he never did. The martyr was intelligent, loyal, brave, and fearless. He was an active member of the American Club and was highly respected. At the beginning of the Shanghai Incident, Japanese planes committed violence. The martyr was indignant and once made a bold statement to his Chinese friends: If I had ten fighter planes, I could drive away the Japanese planes, leaving no armor behind. However, this did not happen, and the martyr was disgruntled for ten days. On February 22, seeing the Japanese planes committing violence in Suzhou, driven by his conscience, he drove a light Boeing fighter plane alone and bravely eliminated the tyranny. He died in the wilderness due to the disparity in numbers. Alas.

Peach Blossoms and Nameless Heroes

— Yan Meng

The wandering train carried my drifting self back to Shanghai from the shores of West Lake, after suffering countless grievances and tasting full of pain. Occasionally, when I think back to the days before the [January 28th Incident], I vaguely feel as if it were another lifetime? When the train suddenly stopped at Longhua, the bright spring sunshine illuminated the peach blossoms of March, which were about to wither. A world of spring was just enough to brush away a bit of bitterness. However, although the spring breeze was so gentle, the fallen petals had long covered the ground. The deep red peach blossoms, in patches, lay on the soil like [mummies], causing people to recall the blood of countless nameless heroes and the struggles of the nation.

If it were not for the [January 28th Incident]'s disaster, which gave the numbed citizens of Shanghai a major shock, and awakened them with the clang of iron and the cry of blood... then I believe that every year, the spring outing ladies, with their carriages like flowing water and horses like dragons, would be jostling and crowding to wander and admire the countless peach blossom groves, with blood wheels smiling and cells smiling as they lingered, forgetting about the [September 18th Incident]? The roar of the storm is like the neighing of warhorses. Friends, if the hot blood in our hearts is still there, and our bones still remain, then we should understand that the radiant spring peach blossoms are about to wither away completely. To continue their charming beauty and the still-existing scenery of Jiangnan, it will depend on the sacrifices of nameless heroes.

The blood of nameless heroes is like the cold and emerald-green of the jasper peach's rouge. The jasper peach is coldly beautiful and lovely, but the blood is warm and moving. Spring has passed in such a way, gone amid the terror of artillery fire. Let our dear young friends close their eyes and think. The Nineteenth Route Army and all the brothers who resisted Japan, their blood is to exchange for the spring sunshine of our future, lying in the spring mud protecting the flowers, waiting for the returning swallows next year to report good news to them. In the future, we no longer want to see the frightening rouge on the lips of Shanghai ladies, we only wish that the young men would all become nameless heroes!

The Shanghai Battle and Military Equipment (18)

— Yi Zang

Searchlights: In the early stages of the World War. Searchlights were used to detect aircraft in the air. At that time, they could only illuminate distances of sixty to ninety *li*. Thus, they did not achieve full effectiveness. By the mid-war period. Searchlights capable of illuminating distances of one hundred fifty *li*, or five or six *gan*, appeared. By 1924. A model with one hundred fifty *li* was invented. Its light source could be protected from the wind and could rotate automatically. Transportation and movement were also extremely convenient. The illumination distance reached six *gan*. Thus, there was no need to worry about night-time defense against enemy aircraft. I heard that the searchlights formerly equipped at the Wusong Fort and the Shizilin Fort could only illuminate three or four *li*. While those used on Japanese warships could reach six *li*. In addition, our army lacked anti-aircraft guns and long-range artillery. The sky was arbitrarily bombed by enemy aircraft. And the sea was unable to prevent enemy ships from advancing. Thinking of national defense. It is truly extremely heartbreaking.

Other equipment for transmitting information. Is the signal used between the air defense surveillance division and the defense headquarters. The relationship is particularly important. Because to prevent enemy aircraft from attacking, we must first pay attention to its actions. Conduct rigorous reconnaissance. If enemy aircraft are seen, regardless of distance, report to all parties immediately. And there must be no errors. For example, when reporting by telephone. Within twenty or thirty seconds. Clearly and accurately convey the information from the surveillance team to the headquarters. Then, there will be no delays. There are also siren devices used to transmit warnings. A Siren can release compressed air and steam to produce a loud sound. Reaching all parties. Recently, portable sirens have been used. In addition to air raid warnings. Infantry units also carry them. When we recall the situation of the Shanghai War this time. What the enemy relied on. Was only airplanes. What our army suffered most from. Was the lack of air force and air defense equipment. In the future, to prepare for the ravages of a great enemy. We must awaken attention to air defense. The most important thing in air defense. Is light control.

Record of Military Life in Shuanglou (33)

— Master Who Seeks Happiness

Chapter 5: Breaking off Friendship and Unfortunately Encountering a Bold Guest; Deciding on a Plan to Endure the Kindness of a Beauty. Speaking of An Yutian's pursuit and questioning of Wei Zhuomou. How could he see that his family's misfortune was caused by his paternal uncle, An Dakui, when his home had been robbed? Wei Zhuomou truthfully recounted all the details detailed in the letter from Mei Village's Mei Zike. It turned out that An Yutian's father was named An Dacheng. He had previously served as an official during the Qing Dynasty, filling several county positions. He accumulated some official wealth. In his old age, he retired to his fields. Because in this Anjia Village. He was considered a great gentry and a famous wealthy man. He was publicly elected as the village head of the entire village. In recent years, the local area has been very unstable. Banditry is rampant everywhere. The mountains are deep and the forests are dense there. The local customs are fierce and bold. And it has always been a gathering place for outlaws. In the area two or three hundred *li* around this Anjia Village. Gangs of bandits with a thousand or eight hundred men are considered large gangs. Gangs of one hundred or several dozen men are considered small gangs. It is already a common sight. Appearing and disappearing unpredictably. It is not considered any kind of rare event. It is only because Anjia Village has historically occupied a very advantageous position. The perimeter of a large village is about ten *li* long. Backed by mountains and close to water. A mud city was built. There is a village gate on each of the four sides, east, south, west, and north. Looking from afar, they are towering and majestic. Like city towers. The earthen gun emplacements are attached to the side of the village towers. Housing more than a dozen old-fashioned red-clad iron cannons. The remaining earthen walls have connected crenellations. Leaving countless gun holes. It is particularly in line with the semi-permanent fortification principles of the new military science. There is a small moat on the southeast side of the city. Connected to the village gate by a drawbridge. The northwest is surrounded by mountains. The terrain is strangely dangerous. The earthen wall snakes like a dragon. Built straight to the mountain peaks. The rear defense is even more solid. Originally, this type of fortress-style village. In their local area. Almost all famous villages and towns are built like this. If not, they cannot protect the peace of their village or town. Inevitably suffering from the attacks of foreign bandits. This has been the custom for a long time. It is the same everywhere. The large and small households in each village and town. As well as various industries and businesses. Must all gather in this type of earthen city with military defense equipment. Outside the city, there are only fields like clouds of paths. Strange and precipitous mountain peaks. And very few scattered dwellings of people. This Anjia Village of his is also the most famous large village. The area is wider than other small villages. The content is especially rich and substantial. In addition to An Dacheng's largest residence. There are still many other brick and tile buildings. Actually connected into one or two very prosperous market streets. Various goods gather. Trade travels through the village. Almost a small county town. Is not as bustling as this. Since it is so prosperous. It inevitably attracts the desires of nearby bandits. Therefore, since An Dacheng took office as village head. He has vigorously increased military preparations. To guard against emergencies. He specially collected a batch of public funds through public donations. Added many new-style firearms. Trained a militia team. Protecting Anjia Village even more like an iron bucket. Determined not to fear any more unexpected foreign attacks.

Local Supplement

Informal Discussions

The Value of Xiao De's Sacrifice

— Gou

When Xiao De died a martyr in Suzhou, I originally intended to write something to express the pain of Xiao De's passing and the greatness of his righteous heroism. However, overwhelmed with emotion and shame, my ink mixed with tears, and I could not write a single word.

Today is the day of Xiao De's public burial. The Xiao De Righteous Martyr Commemoration Committee has made every effort to prepare a grand ceremony to bury him near the Hongqiao Airport to comfort the spirit of Xiao De, the righteous martyr. How could I not say a word to express my condolences and admiration?

Xiao De's sacrifice in Suzhou this time, resisting Japanese aircraft and giving his life, cannot be regarded as merely an ordinary sacrifice due to the war. Xiao De was not acting under the mission of the American government to resist Japan, nor was he acting under the mission of the Chinese government to ask Xiao De to resist Japan. Xiao De's sacrifice this time was entirely his own. Seeing the violent acts of the Japanese army, throwing bombs everywhere and trampling on our people, Xiao De sacrificed purely for world justice and for humanity. This is indeed clear evidence.

Xiao De was an American citizen and had no connection with our country. The Japanese invasion of China had even less to do with Xiao De. However, Xiao De, seeing what was right and acting bravely, disregarded everything and fought bravely against the Japanese aircraft. His courage and determination are commendable. One drop of Xiao De's blood can spread throughout the world, cultivating the flowers of justice and nourishing the fruits of public reason, extending infinitely in all directions, forever shining and indelible.

Therefore, Xiao De's mother said that she had no regrets about the death of her eldest son in China, because he died for international justice and his death was an honor. Indeed, everyone must die, but Xiao De's death is the most meaningful and valuable. Xiao De is not only a righteous man of our country, but also a righteous man of the world, not only a righteous man of the world, but also a model for all mankind. Xiao De's mother has a good son. Here, I respectfully wish the spirit of Xiao De, the righteous martyr, in heaven.

Xiao De sacrificed for world justice and can indeed receive the respect and worship of all our people without shame. However, I wonder what the general traitors who are corrupt officials, the奸商(jian shang) blinded by profit, and the armed classes who embrace non-resistance will think when they see this. What is strange is that when Xiao De's mother arrived in Shanghai, the Americans in Shanghai showed no reaction. Is it because they think that world affairs are not important enough? Alas!

Popular Literature

Ode to Captain Xiao De's Monument

— Meng Tiao Zhu

My friend Mr. Wang has already written a biography of Captain Xiao De's death. Now that Xiao De's mother has come to Shanghai to bury Captain Xiao De's remains at Hongqiao Airport, and various sectors have proposed erecting a monument to Captain Xiao De, I hereby compose this ode to promote its completion.

Thunder and rain seem to convey the urgency of battle, spirits flicker as a lofty monument rises. Towering above the clouds, his bones form a tomb, four hundred million people weep in the rain. At that time, enemy planes came over the river, the killing intent penetrated the blue sky. Innumerable iron bombs were thrown, and the houses below were reduced to flying ash. You, sir, rose up courageously, asking, "What kind of vile creature dares to do this?" The fierce tiger actually flew on wings, "Am I the only one who can bear to sit and watch?" Riding a flying chariot, you pursued the enemy, the enemy's courage failed, and the heavens were astonished. The wind and clouds were trampled upon as you engaged in fierce battle, the mountains shook and the silver sea dazzled. Star officials and flying generals descended from the sky, lightning flashed over the city of Helu. Enemy planes attacked in interlocking formations, how could one plane calmly respond? In an instant, flames annihilated one enemy, and you too were pierced through the chest by a single bullet. The candle dragon fell from the thirty-third heaven, the loyal soul and heroic spirit shattered like glass. Alas, for whom did you die? You sacrificed your life only for justice. Your death is relevant to all living beings; Hua De and Gordon are not worthy of comparison. Your heroic spirit transformed into a rainbow that stretches for thousands of feet, a single rock is enough to be admired. Even now, thunder resounds in the sky of Wu, and spiritual flags and armored horses still come and go. I write a eulogy for your monument, the three words to be engraved are "Peace Monument," one.

Popular Science

Torpedoes

— Xia Ren

Torpedoes are the only effective weapon for bombing warships. They are named for their resemblance to large fish. The head and tail are conical, and the middle is cylindrical, in order to reduce water resistance. The propeller and rudder are at the end, enabling it to move forward automatically in the water, or to be controlled according to a predetermined distance. Recently, they can travel up to 10,000 meters, but the effective range of hitting the target is only about 3,000 meters. In combat, they can be submerged about two feet below the surface of the water so that they are not easily detected by enemy ships. Their value is about nine thousand or more yuan.

Torpedoes were invented in 1866, and the German Whitehead is considered the best. It is fourteen inches in diameter, eleven feet long, weighs three hundred pounds, and contains twenty pounds of explosives. The air pressure of the original power source is 370 pounds per square inch, and the speed is seven knots (now increased to twenty inches in diameter and can hold hundreds of pounds of explosives). It can hit a ship at anchor 400 yards away, and a giant ship underway 200 yards away. At that time, Britain and the United States competed to buy its secrets, not hesitating to spend hundreds of thousands of dollars, but ultimately failed to obtain the German secrets. Therefore, during the European War, Germany used this as the only weapon to defeat the British Navy. The British Navy was blockaded and dared not cross the Lei Pool. The United States joined the Allied Powers because German submarines, disregarding good faith, often used this as an excuse to bomb its merchant ships.

Since then, it has gradually been improved, and a rotary machine has been invented to control its direction, applying the principle of hammer inertia to improve the depth adjustment, and the steel air chamber has been changed to increase the air pressure. All these things cannot be manufactured by our country's military industry. Its structure is roughly as follows:

(1) The head, also known as the warhead, is the chamber for explosives, occupying about a quarter of the total length. It contains a firing pin and a detonator. There are four impellers in the front, which rotate due to water resistance. When a certain distance is reached, the firing pin strikes the detonator to cause the explosion of the explosives. Wet guncotton is used for the explosives, for its safety and strong explosive power. Recently, trilite and similar substances have been used, which are even better because they do not lose their effectiveness even after being immersed in water for several years, and their specific gravity is very large to make up for the lack of explosive power. According to test results, a pressure of 12,000 pounds per square inch on a double-bottomed warship can completely break it. Even if it explodes four feet below the surface of the water, warships twenty feet away will be its victims. When performing exercises, the warhead can be removed and replaced with a dummy head to measure its progress, rocking and depth recording.

(2) The air chamber, occupying half of the total length, is used to store the compressed air of the original power source, about 150 atmospheres. The material must be strong and the work is very important. Its cost accounts for about one-half of the total.

(3) The balance chamber is where the depth adjuster is installed. It has a pendulum and a water pressure plate, which vibrate due to the wave shape. The pendulum swings due to the inclination, and the two interact to control the horizontal rudder.

(4) The engine room is divided into three parts: the engine, the pressure reducing engine, and the steering engine.

(5) The engine mostly uses the Pula-Chahudo cylinder type. The axle passes through the center of the floating chamber to the tail to connect to the two propellers. The compressed air of the original power source is reduced from 150 atmospheres to 30 atmospheres by the pressure reducing valve and enters the engine to start it.

(6) The floating chamber is equipped with a vertical rudder and steering engine to control the left and right deviation of the torpedo.

(7) The car room is equipped with bevel gears to transmit the rotary motion of the engine shaft to the two propellers that react with each other.

(8) The torpedo launch tube, uses gunpowder or compressed air to launch it. The film in the launch tube then causes the torpedo to start and opens the air pipe. Then, air rushes into the various mechanisms and starts the adjusting effect. However, the shaking of the warship has a great impact during launch, and the shaking is often uncontrollable by human power and can reduce the accuracy of the torpedo.

Random Talks

Typical Characters

— Wu

The strong electric light shone through the light blue lampshade, illuminating the magnificent living room like a snowy field. Distinguished guests were being lavishly entertained by the host. The lingering aroma of superior cigars filled the room.

"China is truly amazing, and Shanghai has truly become a free city. Then, we will all be..." the guest said with a hint of emotion.

"Yes, yes, but China is too weak and will never be able to do well. Isn't that right, old friend?" This was the host's smiling reply.

"Exactly, exactly! China is simply too big.

Even if Manchuria were not taken by Japan, it would be seized by Red Russia. Then, rather than letting the Russians communize it, it would be better to let a country with a similar culture coexist and prosper with us."

"That's right! Exactly like that!"

"I heard that the government is going to rely on you again to preside over the finances?"

"Hahaha, there is indeed such news. But you have to treat this specially, old friend," the host said with another complacent laugh.

"Easy to say, easy to say. We're all family. As long as the brothers can continue to operate in the banking sector, we will do our best to help."

"Yes, yes, as the saying goes, 'everyone eats together,' hahaha..."

The sound of mahjong upstairs suddenly stopped, followed by the host's fourth concubine ordering the maid to prepare face water. This made the host very anxious, because it was now time to accompany the fourth concubine to the __ restaurant, so he couldn't help but look troubled and hesitant. Of course, the clever guest was able to understand immediately, cupped his hands, and took his leave with profuse thanks. A moment later, the roar of a car starting its engine was heard in front of the door.

In the house, the host stared at his darling carefully painting her eyebrows, and also surreptitiously pinched her waist while taking a brand new nightgown from the flirtatious maid's hand, and she couldn't help but laugh out loud.

"Hmph! You're stealing chicken again?" This was the concubine's __娇.

"Nothing... Hurry up and get dressed, or we'll be late."

Half an hour later, they were immersed in the warm spring and peaceful, free night air after the war.

East, West, South, North

The Fate of Dong Shi

— You Qi

The afterglow of the setting sun reflected off the corner of the building, dazzlingly dyeing it a reddish-orange color. The gentle breeze blew constantly, and the bustling people wore light clothing to resist the heat bestowed by the season.

In an instant, the afterglow disappeared, and only the scattered electric lights in the urban twilight flickered and illuminated, stirred by the breeze. At this time, in the so-called city center, the flow of people seemed even greater. Some were swallowed into the __楼 or __酒家, some were watching outside the brightly lit glass windows, some were lingering in front of the consignment shops, and some were strolling around aimlessly... Due to the different situations, complex and noisy tones were formed.

"Old Wang, isn't that __路? Hey! The fairies on this road are the most famous."

"Hmph! Forget it, where would there be fairies there? At most, they're just earthly immortals."

"You always affirm things haphazardly without regard for the facts."

"What? You..."

A woman brushed past them.

"Hey! Did you see that? That fat woman?" A Zhu nudged Old Wang with his elbow.

"You're too useless, you're simply like a blind man eating crabs, only knowing that they're good."

After crossing the intersection, on the edge of the sidewalk outside a small alley, a group of women dressed in brightly colored clothes were arranged. Although the light outside the alley was somewhat dim, it could not hinder the delicate whiteness of their faces. "Wang, Wang..." As they passed by them, A Zhu looked straight ahead and whispered.

"Go, go, Dong Shi has opened her mouth."

A Zhu didn't show any reaction, no, perhaps he forgot to react, and continued to stare. Then, they knew, they knew that this was the long-awaited destination that had arrived today, and they rushed up without hesitation.

In the flickering of the dim light, they saw their backs surrounded by several people, being pushed forward as if being tied to the execution ground, disappearing into the narrow alley.

Li Henian and Wu Shiying falsely accuse and appeal (Main Text) The appeal is rejected. The appellant Lin Fengwen and others appeal the case of encroachment (Main Text) All appeals are rejected.

Shanghai Local Court

Criminal Judgment: Zhao Binliang, a case of disturbing order (Main Text) Zhao Binliang, without permission, provided military supplies to the army and is sentenced to one year and six months of imprisonment for the crime. Detention days are commuted to one day of imprisonment for every two days. Two powers of attorney, one blank armband, two symbols, and four books of appointment, etc., are confiscated. Cai Wangshi, an opium case (Main Text) Cai Wangshi is sentenced to six months of imprisonment for transporting opium. Detention days are commuted to one day of imprisonment for every two days. Seventy taels of opium are confiscated and burned. Wu Qiheng sues Zhang Ziheng for fraud (Main Text) Both Wu Qiheng and Zhang Ziheng are innocent. Wang Sanqing and others, a theft case (Main Text) Wang Sanqing and Zhang A'da are each sentenced to eight months of imprisonment for stealing the property of others during a disaster. Detention days are commuted to one day of imprisonment for every two days. (Above, 20th)

Criminal Judgment: Ma Ruifang, an opium case (Main Text) Ma Ruifang is sentenced to one year of imprisonment and fined 200 yuan for transporting opium with the intention of selling it. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment will be commuted for every three yuan. Detention days are commuted to one day of imprisonment for every two days. 176 taels of opium are confiscated and burned. Yang Yunting and others, an opium and gambling case (Main Text) Yang Yunting is sentenced to one year of imprisonment for opening a place for people to smoke opium substitutes with the intention of making a profit. He is fined 30 yuan for the gambling crime, to be executed concurrently. If the fine is not fully paid after compulsory execution, one day of imprisonment will be commuted for every one yuan. Detention days are commuted to one day of imprisonment for every two days. Han Shaoqin, He Agou, and Wu Zhiqi are each sentenced to two months of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. Detention days are commuted to one day of imprisonment for every two days. Qi Dianchang, also known as Qi Jindou, a repeat offender, is sentenced to three months of imprisonment for smoking opium substitutes. Detention days are commuted to one day of imprisonment for every two days. Peng Chengfa is innocent. Four opium pipes, five opium lamps, and sixty red pills are confiscated and burned. Ma Kouzi and others, a robbery case (Main Text) Ma Kouzi, Yu Xiaokouzi, and others, a group of three or more carrying weapons and breaking in to rob, are each sentenced to seven years of imprisonment. Detention days are commuted to one day of imprisonment for every two days.
